Bhagavad Gita - Chapter 18

Read the original Sanskrit shlokas with English, Marathi, and Hindi meanings

‡§∏‡§Ç‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∏‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§Æ‡§π‡§æ‡§¨‡§æ‡§π‡•ã ‡§§‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§ö‡•ç‡§õ‡§æ‡§Æ‡§ø ‡§µ‡•á‡§¶‡§ø‡§§‡•Å‡§Æ‡•ç |
‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ö ‡§π‡•É‡§∑‡•Ä‡§ï‡•á‡§∂ ‡§™‡•É‡§•‡§ï‡•ç‡§ï‡•á‡§∂‡§ø‡§®‡§ø‡§∑‡•Ç‡§¶‡§® || 18.1 ||

English Meaning

Arjuna said: O mighty-armed Krishna, I wish to understand the true nature of renunciation (sannyƒÅsa) and of relinquishment (tyƒÅga), and the difference between them, O Hrishikesha, O Kesava-slayer of the Kesi demon.

Marathi Meaning

‡§Ö‡§∞‡•ç‡§ú‡•Å‡§® ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§π‡§£‡§æ‡§≤‡§æ: ‡§π‡•á ‡§Æ‡§π‡§æ‡§¨‡§æ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ï‡•É‡§∑‡•ç‡§£‡§æ, ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§Ü‡§£‡§ø ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö‡•á ‡§§‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§µ ‡§Æ‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§æ‡§£‡•Ç‡§® ‡§ò‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ø‡§ö‡•á ‡§Ü‡§π‡•á. ‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•É‡§∑‡•Ä‡§ï‡•á‡§∂, ‡§π‡•á ‡§ï‡•á‡§∂‡§ø‡§®‡§ø‡§∑‡•Ç‡§¶‡§®, ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§¶‡•ã‡§ò‡§æ‡§Ç‡§Æ‡§ß‡•Ä‡§≤ ‡§´‡§∞‡§ï ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Ø ‡§Ü‡§π‡•á ‡§§‡•á ‡§Æ‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ó.

Hindi Meaning

‡§Ö‡§∞‡•ç‡§ú‡•Å‡§® ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á: ‡§π‡•á ‡§Æ‡§π‡§æ‡§¨‡§æ‡§π‡•Å ‡§ï‡•É‡§∑‡•ç‡§£! ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§§‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§µ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å, ‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•É‡§∑‡•Ä‡§ï‡•á‡§∂! ‡§π‡•á ‡§ï‡•á‡§∂‡§ø‡§®‡§ø‡§∑‡•Ç‡§¶‡§®! ‡§ï‡•É‡§™‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§¶‡•ã‡§®‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§§‡§∞ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§¨‡§§‡§æ‡§á‡§è‡•§

‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§≠‡§ó‡§µ‡§æ‡§®‡•Å‡§µ‡§æ‡§ö |
‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§®‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§£‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∏‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∏‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§µ‡§Ø‡•ã ‡§µ‡§ø‡§¶‡•Å‡§É |
‡§∏‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§´‡§≤‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡§Ç ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§π‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡§Ç ‡§µ‡§ø‡§ö‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§£‡§æ‡§É || 18.2 ||

English Meaning

The Blessed Lord said: The sages understand sannyƒÅsa as the renunciation of actions done with desire; the wise declare the abandonment of the fruits of all actions as tyƒÅga.

Marathi Meaning

‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§≠‡§ó‡§µ‡§æ‡§® ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§π‡§£‡§æ‡§≤‡•á: ‡§ú‡•ç‡§û‡§æ‡§®‡•Ä ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ï ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§π‡§£‡§ú‡•á ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§Ö‡§∏‡•á ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§π‡§£‡§§‡§æ‡§§; ‡§§‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§´‡§≥‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§π‡§£‡§ú‡•á ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Ö‡§∏‡•á ‡§µ‡§ø‡§µ‡•á‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ï ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ó‡§§‡§æ‡§§.

Hindi Meaning

‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§≠‡§ó‡§µ‡§æ‡§® ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á: ‡§ú‡•ç‡§û‡§æ‡§®‡•Ä‡§ú‡§® ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§π‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§´‡§≤‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§π‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Ç ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∑‡§µ‡§¶‡§ø‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡•á‡§ï‡•á ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§π‡•Å‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§®‡•Ä‡§∑‡§ø‡§£‡§É |
‡§Ø‡§ú‡•ç‡§û‡§¶‡§æ‡§®‡§§‡§™‡§É‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§® ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Æ‡§ø‡§§‡§ø ‡§ö‡§æ‡§™‡§∞‡•á || 18.3 ||

English Meaning

Some philosophers declare that action should be given up as evil, while others say that acts of sacrifice, charity, and penance should not be abandoned.

Marathi Meaning

‡§ï‡§æ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§µ‡§ø‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞‡§µ‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∑‡§Ø‡•Å‡§ï‡•ç‡§§ ‡§Ü‡§π‡•á ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§π‡§£‡•Ç‡§® ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ö‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡§æ‡§µ‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§∏‡•á ‡§Æ‡•ç‡§π‡§£‡§§‡§æ‡§§; ‡§§‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§π‡•Ä‡§ú‡§£ ‡§Ø‡§ú‡•ç‡§û, ‡§¶‡§æ‡§® ‡§Ü‡§£‡§ø ‡§§‡§™ ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç ‡§®‡§Ø‡•á ‡§Ö‡§∏‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ó‡§§‡§æ‡§§.

Hindi Meaning

‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ ‡§ú‡•ç‡§û‡§æ‡§®‡•Ä‡§ú‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∑‡§Ø‡•Å‡§ï‡•ç‡§§ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ï‡§π‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§ú‡§¨‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ö‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó ‡§Ø‡§ú‡•ç‡§û, ‡§¶‡§æ‡§® ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§§‡§™ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è, ‡§ê‡§∏‡§æ ‡§ï‡§π‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

‡§®‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§Ø‡§Ç ‡§∂‡•É‡§£‡•Å ‡§Æ‡•á ‡§§‡§§‡•ç‡§∞ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡•á ‡§≠‡§∞‡§§‡§∏‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡§Æ |
‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡•ã ‡§π‡§ø ‡§™‡•Å‡§∞‡•Å‡§∑‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ò‡•ç‡§∞ ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§µ‡§ø‡§ß‡§É ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡•Ä‡§∞‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§§‡§É || 18.4 ||

English Meaning

Hear from Me the truth about renunciation, O best of the Bharatas! Renunciation, O tiger among men, has been declared to be of three kinds.

Marathi Meaning

‡§π‡•á ‡§≠‡§∞‡§§‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§∑‡•ç‡§†, ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡§æ‡§¨‡§¶‡•ç‡§¶‡§≤ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ù‡•á ‡§®‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§ø‡§§ ‡§Æ‡§§ ‡§ê‡§ï. ‡§π‡•á ‡§™‡•Å‡§∞‡•Å‡§∑‡§∏‡§ø‡§Ç‡§π, ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§π‡§æ ‡§§‡•Ä‡§® ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§ö‡§æ ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ó‡§ø‡§§‡§≤‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§π‡•á.

Hindi Meaning

‡§π‡•á ‡§≠‡§∞‡§§‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§∑‡•ç‡§†! ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡•á ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∑‡§Ø ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡§æ ‡§®‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§ø‡§§ ‡§Æ‡§§ ‡§∏‡•Å‡§®‡•ã‡•§ ‡§π‡•á ‡§™‡•Å‡§∞‡•Å‡§∑‡§∏‡§ø‡§Ç‡§π! ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§§‡•Ä‡§® ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ ‡§ó‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

‡§Ø‡§ú‡•ç‡§û‡§¶‡§æ‡§®‡§§‡§™‡§É‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§® ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Æ‡•á‡§µ ‡§§‡§§‡•ç |
‡§Ø‡§ú‡•ç‡§û‡•ã ‡§¶‡§æ‡§®‡§Ç ‡§§‡§™‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡•à‡§µ ‡§™‡§æ‡§µ‡§®‡§æ‡§®‡§ø ‡§Æ‡§®‡•Ä‡§∑‡§ø‡§£‡§æ‡§Æ‡•ç || 18.5 ||

English Meaning

Acts of sacrifice, charity, and penance are not to be given up; they must be performed. Indeed, sacrifice, charity, and penance are purifying even for those who are wise.

Marathi Meaning

‡§Ø‡§ú‡•ç‡§û, ‡§¶‡§æ‡§® ‡§Ü‡§£‡§ø ‡§§‡§™ ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç ‡§®‡§Ø‡•á; ‡§§‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§∞‡§£‡•á ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§∂‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï ‡§Ü‡§π‡•á. ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§£ ‡§π‡•á ‡§ú‡•ç‡§û‡§æ‡§®‡•Ä ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ï‡§æ‡§Ç‡§∏‡§æ‡§†‡•Ä‡§π‡•Ä ‡§™‡§æ‡§µ‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡§£‡§æ‡§∞‡•á ‡§Ü‡§π‡•á‡§§.

Hindi Meaning

‡§Ø‡§ú‡•ç‡§û, ‡§¶‡§æ‡§® ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§§‡§™ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è; ‡§Ø‡•á ‡§Ö‡§µ‡§∂‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ø‡•á ‡§ú‡•ç‡§û‡§æ‡§®‡•Ä‡§ú‡§®‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§™‡§µ‡§ø‡§§‡•ç‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

‡§è‡§§‡§æ‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§™‡§ø ‡§§‡•Å ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§£‡§ø ‡§∏‡§ô‡•ç‡§ó‡§Ç ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ ‡§´‡§≤‡§æ‡§®‡§ø ‡§ö |
‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§§‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§®‡•Ä‡§§‡§ø ‡§Æ‡•á ‡§™‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§• ‡§®‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§ø‡§§‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡§§‡§Æ‡•Å‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡§Æ‡§Æ‡•ç || 18.6 ||

English Meaning

Even these actions should be performed by giving up attachment and the desire for rewards, O Arjuna. This is My definite and supreme verdict.

Marathi Meaning

‡§π‡•á ‡§™‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§•, ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§∏‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§Ç‡§®‡§æ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§∏‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§£‡§ø ‡§´‡§≥‡§æ‡§ö‡•Ä ‡§á‡§ö‡•ç‡§õ‡§æ ‡§® ‡§†‡•á‡§µ‡§§‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§æ‡§µ‡•á, ‡§π‡•á ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ù‡•á ‡§®‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§ø‡§§ ‡§Ü‡§£‡§ø ‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§∑‡•ç‡§† ‡§Æ‡§§ ‡§Ü‡§π‡•á.

Hindi Meaning

‡§π‡•á ‡§™‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§•! ‡§á‡§® ‡§∏‡§¨ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§∏‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§´‡§≤ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§á‡§ö‡•ç‡§õ‡§æ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡§ï‡•á ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‚Äî‡§Ø‡§π ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡§æ ‡§®‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§ø‡§§ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§∑‡•ç‡§† ‡§Æ‡§§ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§§‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§§‡•Å ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∏‡§É ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§£‡•ã ‡§®‡•ã‡§™‡§™‡§¶‡•ç‡§Ø‡§§‡•á |
‡§Æ‡•ã‡§π‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§™‡§∞‡§ø‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡§æ‡§Æ‡§∏‡§É ‡§™‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï‡•Ä‡§∞‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§§‡§É || 18.7 ||

English Meaning

But the renunciation of prescribed duties is not proper. Abandoning such work out of delusion is declared to be in the mode of ignorance (tamas).

Marathi Meaning

‡§™‡§∞‡§Ç‡§§‡•Å ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§®‡§æ‡§π‡•Ä. ‡§Æ‡•ã‡§π‡§æ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§≥‡•á ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡§£‡•á ‡§π‡§æ ‡§§‡§æ‡§Æ‡§∏ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§ú‡§≤‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•ã.

Hindi Meaning

‡§ï‡§ø‡§®‡•ç‡§§‡•Å ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§â‡§ö‡§ø‡§§ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•ã‡§π‡§µ‡§∂ ‡§â‡§®‡§ï‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§§‡§æ‡§Æ‡§∏ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ ‡§ó‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

‡§¶‡•Å‡§É‡§ñ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡•á‡§µ ‡§Ø‡§§‡•ç‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§≤‡•á‡§∂‡§≠‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ú‡•á‡§§‡•ç |
‡§∏ ‡§ï‡•É‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§∏‡§Ç ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡§Ç ‡§®‡•à‡§µ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡§´‡§≤‡§Ç ‡§≤‡§≠‡•á‡§§‡•ç || 18.8 ||

English Meaning

He who abandons prescribed duty because it is troublesome or out of fear of bodily discomfort, does so in the mode of passion (rajas) and does not gain the merit of renunciation.

Marathi Meaning

‡§ú‡•ã ‡§Æ‡§®‡•Å‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡•á‡§µ‡§≥ ‡§ï‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ç‡§µ‡§æ ‡§∂‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï ‡§µ‡•á‡§¶‡§®‡•á‡§ö‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§≠‡•Ä‡§§‡•Ä‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ö‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•ã, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§∏ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§≤‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§£‡§ø ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§≤‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡§æ‡§ö‡•á ‡§´‡§≥ ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§≥‡§§ ‡§®‡§æ‡§π‡•Ä.

Hindi Meaning

‡§ú‡•ã ‡§Æ‡§®‡•Å‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡•á‡§µ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§∂‡§∞‡•Ä‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡•Ä‡§°‡§º‡§æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≠‡§Ø ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§µ‡§π ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§∏ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§π‡§≤‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§â‡§∏‡•á ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§´‡§≤ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§≤‡§§‡§æ‡•§

‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Æ‡§ø‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡•á‡§µ ‡§Ø‡§§‡•ç‡§ï‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§§‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§§‡•á‡§Ω‡§∞‡•ç‡§ú‡•Å‡§® |
‡§∏‡§ô‡•ç‡§ó‡§Ç ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ ‡§´‡§≤‡§Ç ‡§ö‡•à‡§µ ‡§∏ ‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ó‡§É ‡§∏‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡§ø‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Æ‡§§‡§É || 18.9 ||

English Meaning

O Arjuna, when one performs prescribed duty simply because it ought to be done, abandoning attachment and desire for rewards, such renunciation is regarded as sattvic (in the mode of goodness).

Marathi Meaning

English Meaning

Knowledge, the object of knowledge, and the knower‚Äîthese are the threefold impetus to action; the instrument, the action, and the doer are the threefold constituents of action.

English Meaning

Knowledge, action, and the doer are declared in the philosophy of the gunas (qualities) to be of three kinds according to the modes of nature. Hear about them as well.

English Meaning

That knowledge by which one sees the one imperishable reality in all beings, undivided in the divided, know that knowledge to be sattvic (in the mode of goodness).

English Meaning

But that knowledge which sees in all beings various entities of different kinds as separate from one another, know that knowledge to be rajasic (in the mode of passion).

English Meaning

But that knowledge which clings to one single effect as if it were the whole, without reason and without understanding the truth, and which is trivial‚Äîsuch knowledge is declared to be tamasic (in the mode of ignorance).

English Meaning

Action that is prescribed, performed without attachment, without love or hatred, and without desire for results, is said to be sattvic (in the mode of goodness).

But action performed with great effort by one seeking to gratify desires, or with a sense of ego, is declared to be rajasic (in the mode of passion).

English Meaning

That action which is undertaken from delusion, without regard for consequences, loss, injury, or one's own ability, is said to be tamasic (in the mode of ignorance).

English Meaning

And remembering again and again that most wonderful form of Hari, great is my amazement, O King, and I rejoice again and again.

‡§§‡§§‡•ç‡§∞ ‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ‡§ø‡§ú‡§Ø‡•ã ‡§≠‡•Ç‡§§‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§ß‡•ç‡§∞‡•Å‡§µ‡§æ ‡§®‡•Ä‡§§‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§§‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§Æ || 18.78 ||

English Meaning

Wherever there is Krishna, the Lord of Yoga, and Arjuna, the wielder of the bow, there will surely be fortune, victory, prosperity, and sound morality; such is my conviction.

Marathi Meaning
